  member this.prime100 =

      | [] -> [] 
      | h::t -> h::primes(List.filter (fun x->x%h>0) t) 
    primes [2..100] |> List.fold(fun x y -> x+","+y.ToString()) "" 
                                |> fun x-> x.Substring(1) </script>

mov RBP,RSP
sub RSP,020h
mov -018h[RBP],RBX
movsd -8[RBP],XMM0
movsd XMM1,-8[RBP]
movsd -010h[RBP],XMM1
